´ïf.a kshufhka

3 = I (R1 + R2)

Bys úNjh VB kï" R2 yryd úNj wka;rh VB fõ'

∴ I = 3R1 + R2

V = IR

VB = R2 × 3R1 + R2

VB = R2 I

●R1 ksh; j ;nd R2 fjkia lsÍfuka 0 isg 3 V olajd ´kE u úNjhla tu ,laIHhg ,nd Èh yels h'

●R1 = 10 kΩ kï VB = 0.7 V ùug R2ys w.h fidhuq'

3 × R210,000 + R20.7 =

7000 + 0.7 R2 = 3 × R27000 = 3 × R2 - 0.7 R2 = 2.3 R2

∴ R2 = 2.37000 = 3043 Ω

∴ R2 ys w.h 3043 Ω jq úg Bys úNjh 0.7 V fõ'
